class="contentItem__contentWrapper"><p class="contentItem__subhead contentItem__subhead--shortstop">The Dodgers jumped out to a big early lead and withstood a mid-game longball outburst by the Diamondbacks, taking Game 1 of the NLDS 9-5 on Friday. He struck out seven and allowed just five hits, but four of Arizona's hits against him were solo homers.
